function PcldOwner()
	task.spawn(function()
		while task.wait(0.1) do
			usedNames = {};
			for v1969, v1970 in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
				if (v1970.Name == "PlayerCharacterLocationDetector") then
					if (v1970.CFrame == CFrame.new(0, 0, 0, 1, 0, 0, 0, 1, 0, 0, 0, 1)) then
						continue;
					end
					hasOwner = false;
					existingBoolValues = {};
					for v3007, v3008 in pairs(v1970:GetChildren()) do
						if v3008:IsA("BoolValue") then
							table.insert(existingBoolValues, v3008);
						end
					end
					if (#existingBoolValues >= 2) then
						for v3373, v3374 in pairs(existingBoolValues) do
							v3374:Destroy();
						end
					elseif (#existingBoolValues == 1) then
						hasOwner = true;
					end
					if hasOwner then
						continue;
					end
					closestPlayer = nil;
					closestDist = 30;
					candidates = {};
					for v3009, v3010 in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
						if (v3010.Character and v3010.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")) then
							hrp = v3010.Character.HumanoidRootPart;
							dist = (v1970.Position - hrp.Position).Magnitude;
							if (dist < closestDist) then
								table.insert(candidates, {player=v3010,dist=dist,hrp=hrp});
							end
						end
					end
					table.sort(candidates, function(v3011, v3012)
						return v3011.dist < v3012.dist;
					end);
					for v3013, v3014 in pairs(candidates) do
						ownerName = string.format("[ %s ] ( @%s )", v3014.player.DisplayName, v3014.player.Name);
						if not usedNames[ownerName] then
							closestPlayer = v3014.player;
							closestDist = v3014.dist;
							usedNames[ownerName] = true;
							break;
						end
					end
					if closestPlayer then
						ownerName = string.format("[ %s ] ( @%s )", closestPlayer.DisplayName, closestPlayer.Name);
						boolValue = nil;
						for v3380, v3381 in pairs(v1970:GetChildren()) do
							if v3381:IsA("BoolValue") then
								boolValue = v3381;
								boolValue.Name = ownerName;
								break;
							end
						end
						if not boolValue then
							boolValue = Instance.new("BoolValue");
							boolValue.Name = ownerName;
							boolValue.Parent = v1970;
						end
						task.spawn(function(v3382, v3383)
							while v3383.Parent do
								if (v3382.Character and v3382.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")) then
									hrp = v3382.Character.HumanoidRootPart;
									if (hrp.Massless == true) then
										if not v3383.Value then
											v3383.Value = true;
										end
									elseif v3383.Value then
										v3383.Value = false;
									end
									if (not Players:FindFirstChild(v3382.Name) or not v3382.Character or (v3382.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and (v3382.Character.Humanoid.Health <= 0))) then
										v3383:Destroy();
										break;
									end
								else
									v3383:Destroy();
									break;
								end
								task.wait(0.1);
							end
						end, closestPlayer, boolValue);
					end
				end
			end
		end
	end);
end
function SpawnCFrame()
	local v199;
	myDisplayName = plr.DisplayName;
	myUserName = plr.Name;
	myPOIdentifier = string.format("[ %s ] ( @%s )", myDisplayName, myUserName);
	function findMyPO()
		for v1548, v1549 in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
			if (v1549.Name == "PlayerCharacterLocationDetector") then
				for v2722, v2723 in pairs(v1549:GetChildren()) do
					if (v2723:IsA("BoolValue") and (v2723.Name == myPOIdentifier)) then
						return v1549;
					end
				end
			end
		end
		return nil;
	end
	if (not workspace:FindFirstChild("CamPart") or workspace:FindFirstChild("CamPart"):FindFirstChild("CamPart")) then
		char = plr.Character or plr.CharacterAdded:Wait();
		v199 = char:FindFirstChild("CamPart"):Clone();
		v199.Name = "CamPart";
		v199.Parent = workspace;
		v199.Transparency = 0.9;
	else
		v199 = workspace.CamPart;
	end
	lastHRPVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0);
	task.spawn(function()
		rayParams = RaycastParams.new();
		rayParams.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Exclude;
		while true do
			ping = plr:GetNetworkPing();
			myPO = findMyPO();
			char = plr.Character;
			hrp = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
			if hrp then
				lastHRPVelocity = hrp.Velocity;
			end
			if (myPO and hrp) then
				rayParams.FilterDescendantsInstances = {char,v199,myPO};
				offset = myPO.Position + (lastHRPVelocity * (ping + 0.15));
				rayOrigin = offset;
				rayDirection = Vector3.new(0, 23, 0);
				rayResult = workspace:Raycast(rayOrigin, rayDirection, rayParams);
				v2[1246] = nil;
				if rayResult then
					v2[1246] = rayResult.Position - Vector3.new(0, 0.5, 0);
				else
					v2[1246] = offset + rayDirection;
				end
				originalRotation = myPO.CFrame.Rotation * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-90), 0, 0);
				v199.CFrame = CFrame.new(v2[1246]) * originalRotation;
				rayParams.FilterDescendantsInstances = {char,v199};
				offset = hrp.Position + (lastHRPVelocity * (ping + 0.15));
				rayOrigin = offset;
				rayDirection = Vector3.new(0, 20, 0);
				rayResult = workspace:Raycast(rayOrigin, rayDirection, rayParams);
				v2[1371] = nil;
				if rayResult then
					v2[1371] = rayResult.Position - Vector3.new(0, 0.5, 0);
				else
					v2[1371] = offset + rayDirection;
				end
				originalRotation = (hrp.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-90), 0, 0)).Rotation;
				v199.CFrame = CFrame.new(v2[1371]) * originalRotation;
				v199.Name = "SpawnCF";
			end
			task.wait();
		end
	end);
	return v199;
end

function House()
	char = plr.Character;
	if not char then
		Plot = nil;
		return;
	end
	if (char.Parent and (char.Parent.Name == "PlayersInPlots")) then
		for v1973, v1974 in workspace.Plots:GetChildren() do
			for v2490, v2491 in v1974.PlotSign.ThisPlotsOwners:GetChildren() do
				if (v2491.Value == plr.Name) then
					if (v1974.Name == "Plot1") then
						Plot = 1;
					elseif (v1974.Name == "Plot2") then
						Plot = 2;
					elseif (v1974.Name == "Plot3") then
						Plot = 3;
					elseif (v1974.Name == "Plot4") then
						Plot = 4;
					elseif (v1974.Name == "Plot5") then
						Plot = 5;
					end
					return;
				end
			end
		end
		Plot = nil;
		return;
	end
	if ((char.Parent == workspace) or (char.Parent == inv)) then
		for v1975, v1976 in workspace.Plots:GetChildren() do
			for v2492, v2493 in v1976.PlotSign.ThisPlotsOwners:GetChildren() do
				if (v2493.Value == plr.Name) then
					if (v1976.Name == "Plot1") then
						Plot = 1;
					elseif (v1976.Name == "Plot2") then
						Plot = 2;
					elseif (v1976.Name == "Plot3") then
						Plot = 3;
					elseif (v1976.Name == "Plot4") then
						Plot = 4;
					elseif (v1976.Name == "Plot5") then
						Plot = 5;
					end
					return;
				end
			end
		end
		Plot = nil;
	else
		Plot = nil;
	end
end
function UpdateCurrentBlobman()
	char = plr.Character;
	hrp = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
	if not hrp then
		return;
	end
	for v1081, v1082 in workspace:GetDescendants() do
		if (v1082.Name ~= "CreatureBlobman") then
			continue;
		end
		seat = v1082:FindFirstChild("VehicleSeat");
		if not seat then
			continue;
		end
		weld = seat:FindFirstChild("SeatWeld");
		if not weld then
			continue;
		end
		if (weld.Part1 == hrp) then
			currentBlobS = v1082;
		end
	end
end

function flingF()
	workspace.ChildAdded:Connect(function(v1083)
		if (v1083.Name == "GrabParts") then
			part_to_impulse = v1083['GrabPart']['WeldConstraint'].Part1;
			if part_to_impulse then
				v1083:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Parent"):Connect(function()
					if (not v1083.Parent and flingT) then
						local v3384;
						v3384 = uis.InputBegan:Connect(function(v3491, v3492)
							if (v3491.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton2) then
								velocityObj = Instance.new("BodyVelocity");
								velocityObj.Parent = part_to_impulse;
								velocityObj.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge);
								velocityObj.Velocity = cam.CFrame.lookVector * strengthV;
								wait(0.1);
								velocityObj.Parent = workspace;
								velocityObj:Destroy();
								v3384:Disconnect();
							end
						end);
					end
				end);
			end
		end
	end);
end
function infLineExtendF()
	uis.InputChanged:Connect(function(v1084)
		if (v1084.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseWheel) then
			if (lineDistanceV < 11) then
				lineDistanceV = 11;
			end
			if (v1084.Position.Z > 0) then
				lineDistanceV = lineDistanceV + increaseLineExtendV;
			elseif (v1084.Position.Z < 0) then
				lineDistanceV = lineDistanceV - increaseLineExtendV;
			end
		end
	end);
	workspace.ChildAdded:Connect(function(v1085)
		if ((v1085.Name == "GrabParts") and v1085:IsA("Model")) then
			if (infLineExtendT and uis.MouseEnabled) then
				grabPartsModel = v1085;
				grabPartsModel:WaitForChild("GrabPart");
				grabPartsModel:WaitForChild("DragPart");
				clonedDragPart = grabPartsModel.DragPart:Clone();
				clonedDragPart.Name = "DragPart1";
				clonedDragPart.AlignPosition.Attachment1 = clonedDragPart.DragAttach;
				clonedDragPart.Parent = grabPartsModel;
				lineDistanceV = (clonedDragPart.Position - cam.CFrame.Position).Magnitude;
				clonedDragPart.AlignOrientation.Enabled = false;
				grabPartsModel.DragPart.AlignPosition.Enabled = false;
				if MasslessGrabT then
					alignOrientation = clonedDragPart:FindFirstChildOfClass("AlignOrientation");
					if alignOrientation then
						alignOrientation.MaxAngularVelocity = math.huge;
						alignOrientation.MaxTorque = math.huge;
						alignOrientation.Responsiveness = 200;
					end
					alignPosition = clonedDragPart:FindFirstChildOfClass("AlignPosition");
					if alignPosition then
						alignPosition.MaxAxesForce = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge);
						alignPosition.MaxForce = math.huge;
						alignPosition.MaxVelocity = math.huge;
						alignPosition.Responsiveness = 200;
					end
				end
				task.spawn(function()
					while grabPartsModel.Parent do
						clonedDragPart.Position = cam.CFrame.Position + (cam.CFrame.LookVector * lineDistanceV);
						task.wait();
					end
					lineDistanceV = 0;
				end);
			end
		end
	end);
end

function updateWalkSpeedF()
	function apply(v1094)
		hum = v1094:WaitForChild("Humanoid");

			hum.WalkSpeed = walkSpeedV;
			hum:GetPropertyChangedSignal("WalkSpeed"):Connect(function()
				if walkSpeedT then
					hum.WalkSpeed = walkSpeedV;
				end
			end);
		else
			hum.WalkSpeed = 16;
		end
	end
	if plr.Character then
		apply(plr.Character);
	end
	plr.CharacterAdded:Connect(apply);
end

RunService = game:GetService("RunService");
NO_CLIP_PARTS = {"Head","Torso","Left Arm","Left Leg","Right Arm","Right Leg"};
function updateNoClipF()
	char = plr.Character;
	if not char then
		return;
	end
	if noClipConnection then
		noClipConnection:Disconnect();
		noClipConnection = nil;
	end
	if not noClipT then
		restoreCollision(char);
		return;
	end
	hrp = char:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart");
	hum = char:WaitForChild("Humanoid");
	noClipConnection = RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
		if (not noClipT or not char or not char.Parent) then
			if noClipConnection then
				noClipConnection:Disconnect();
				noClipConnection = nil;
			end
			return;
		end
		for v1555, v1556 in ipairs(NO_CLIP_PARTS) do
			part = char:FindFirstChild(v1556);
			if (part and part:IsA("BasePart")) then
				part.CanCollide = false;
			end
		end
	end);
end
function restoreCollision(v218)
	if v218 then
		for v1982, v1983 in ipairs(NO_CLIP_PARTS) do
			part = v218:FindFirstChild(v1983);
			if (part and part:IsA("BasePart")) then
				part.CanCollide = true;
			end
		end
	end
end
plr.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(v219)
	v219:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart");
	task.wait(0.5);
	if noClipT then
		updateNoClipF();
	end
end);
if plr.Character then
	task.wait(1);
	if noClipT then
		updateNoClipF();
	end
end
function updateInfJumpF()
	char = plr.Character;
	if not char then
		return;
	end
	hrp = char:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart");
	hum = char:WaitForChild("Humanoid");
	if infJumpConnection then
		infJumpConnection:Disconnect();
	end
	infJumpConnection = uis.JumpRequest:Connect(function()
		if (infJumpT and not infJumpD) then
			infJumpD = true;
			hum:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Jumping);
			task.wait();
			infJumpD = true;
		end
	end);
end
plr.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(v221)
	v221:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart");
	v221:WaitForChild("Humanoid");
	task.wait(0.5);
	if infJumpT then
		updateInfJumpF();
	end
end);
if plr.Character then
	task.wait(1);
	updateInfJumpF();
end
function masslessF()
	function applyMassless(v1096)
		hrp = v1096:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart");
		hum = v1096:WaitForChild("Humanoid");
		if masslessT then
			task.spawn(function()
				while masslessT and v1096.Parent do
					for v3021, v3022 in ipairs(v1096:GetChildren()) do
						if v3022:IsA("BasePart") then
							v3022.Massless = false;
						end
					end
					task.wait();
				end
			end);
		end
	end
	if plr.Character then
		applyMassless(plr.Character);
	end
	plr.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(v1097)
		task.wait(1);
		applyMassless(v1097);
	end);
end
function setRagdollF(v222)
	char = plr.Character;
	hrp = char:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart");
	if (char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")) then
		rs.CharacterEvents.RagdollRemote:FireServer(hrp, (v222 and 1) or 0);
	end
end
function permRagdollLoopF()
	if permRagdollRunningS then
		return;
	end
	permRagdollRunningS = true;
	while permRagdollT do

function ragdollLegExplodeF()
	function attemptDelete()
		char = plr.Character;
		if not char then
			return false;
		end
		targets = {};
		if (selectedAutoDeletePart == "Arm/Leg") then
			targets = {char:FindFirstChild("Left Leg"),char:FindFirstChild("Right Leg"),char:FindFirstChild("Left Arm"),char:FindFirstChild("Right Arm")};
		elseif (selectedAutoDeletePart == "All/Leg") then
			targets = {char:FindFirstChild("Left Leg"),char:FindFirstChild("Right Leg")};
		elseif (selectedAutoDeletePart == "Leg/왼쪽") then
			targets = {char:FindFirstChild("Left Leg")};
		elseif (selectedAutoDeletePart == "Leg/오른쪽") then
			targets = {char:FindFirstChild("Right Leg")};
		elseif (selectedAutoDeletePart == "All/Arm") then
			targets = {char:FindFirstChild("Left Arm"),char:FindFirstChild("Right Arm")};
		elseif (selectedAutoDeletePart == "Arm/왼쪽") then
			targets = {char:FindFirstChild("Left Arm")};
		elseif (selectedAutoDeletePart == "Arm/오른쪽") then
			targets = {char:FindFirstChild("Right Arm")};
		end
		setRagdollF(true);
		task.wait(0.3);
		success = false;
		for v1557, v1558 in ipairs(targets) do
			if v1558 then
				v1558.CFrame = CFrame.new(0, -99999, 0);
				success = true;
			end
		end
		task.wait(0.3);
		torso = char:FindFirstChild("Torso");
		if torso then
			torso.CFrame = CFrame.new(0, -99999, 0);
		end
		return success;
	end
	task.spawn(function()
		while autoDeleteLegs do
			success = false;
			startTime = tick();
			while ((tick() - startTime) < 4) and not success do
				success = attemptDelete();
				if success then
					break;
				end
				task.wait(0.5);
			end
			humanoid = plr.Character and plr.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid");
			if humanoid then
				humanoid.Died:Wait();
			end
			plr.CharacterAdded:Wait();
			task.wait(1);
		end
	end);
end
Pline = rs.GrabEvents.CreateGrabLine.OnClientEvent;
fireCount = {};
function AntiLagF()
	Pline:Connect(function(v1099, ...)
		if not antiLagEnabled then
			return;
		end
		if ((typeof(v1099) ~= "Instance") or not v1099:IsA("Player")) then
			return;
		end
		if (v1099 == plr) then
			return;
		end
		v2[4140] = os.clock();
		if not fireCount[v1099] then
			fireCount[v1099] = {count=0,start=v2[4140]};
		end
		local v1101 = fireCount[v1099];
		if ((v2[4140] - v1101.start) > 1) then
			v1101.count = 0;
			v1101.start = v2[4140];
		end
		v1101.count += 1
		if ((v1101.count >= AntiLagV) and not v1101.isDecreasing) then
			v1101.isDecreasing = true;
			v6:Notify({Title="[ ✏️ ]",Content=("by: " .. v1099.Name),Duration=3,Image=0});
			plr.PlayerScripts.CharacterAndBeamMove.Enabled = false;
			task.spawn(function()
				while v1101.count > 0 do
					task.wait(0.1);
					v1101.count -= 1
				end
				plr.PlayerScripts.CharacterAndBeamMove.Enabled = true;
				fireCount[v1099] = nil;
			end);
		end
	end);
end

function spawnBlobmanF()
	char = plr.Character;
	hrp = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
	if not hrp then
		return;
	end
	blob = inv and inv:FindFirstChild("CreatureBlobman");
	if blob then
		blobmanInstanceS = blob;
		return;
	end
	spawnRemote = rs:FindFirstChild("MenuToys") and rs.MenuToys:FindFirstChild("SpawnToyRemoteFunction");
	if spawnRemote then
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				spawnRemote:InvokeServer("CreatureBlobman", hrp.CFrame, Vector3.new(0, 0, 0));
			end);
		end);
		tries = 0;
		repeat
			task.wait(0.02);
			blobmanInstanceS = inv and inv:FindFirstChild("CreatureBlobman");
			tries += 1
		until blobmanInstanceS or (tries > 25) 
	else
	end
end
function ragdollLoopF()
	if ragdollLoopD then
		return;
	end
	ragdollLoopD = true;
	while sitJumpT do
		char = plr.Character;
		hrp = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
		if (char and hrp) then
			args = {[1]=hrp,[2]=0};
			remote = rs:FindFirstChild("CharacterEvents") and rs.CharacterEvents:FindFirstChild("RagdollRemote");
			if remote then
				remote:FireServer(unpack(args));
			end
		end
		task.wait();
	end
	ragdollLoopD = false;
end
function sitJumpF()
	char = plr.Character;
	hum = char and char:FindFirstChild("Humanoid");
	if (not char or not hum) then
		return;
	end
	seat = blobmanInstanceS and blobmanInstanceS:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("VehicleSeat");
	if (seat and (seat.Occupant ~= hum)) then
		seat:Sit(hum);
		autoGucciT = false;
		sitJumpT = false;
	end
end
function AutoGucciF()
	while AutoGucciT do
		v2[4786] = pcall(function()
			spawnBlobmanF();
			char = plr.Character;
			if not char then
				task.wait(0.2);
				return;
			end
			hrp = char:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart");
			hum = char:WaitForChild("Humanoid");
			rag = hum:WaitForChild("Ragdolled");
			held = plr:WaitForChild("IsHeld");
			SpawnToyRemoteFunction = RepStorage.MenuToys.SpawnToyRemoteFunction;
			RagdollRemote = RepStorage.CharacterEvents.RagdollRemote;
			DestroyToy = RepStorage.MenuToys.DestroyToy;
			seat = blobmanInstanceS:WaitForChild("VehicleSeat"):WaitForChild("ProximityPrompt");
			if not hrp then
				return;
			end
			OCF = hrp.CFrame;
			if not sitJumpT then
				task.spawn(sitJumpF);
				sitJumpT = true;
			end
			task.spawn(ragdollLoopF);
			task.wait(0.3);
			hrp.CFrame = OCF;
			successCheck = true;
			sitJumpT = false;
			RagdollRemote:FireServer(hrp, 0.001);
			while successCheck and AutoGucciT do
				if (hum.Health <= 0) then
					if blobmanInstanceS then
						DestroyToy:FireServer(blobmanInstanceS);
					end
					successCheck = false;
					break;
				end
				seat = blobmanInstanceS and blobmanInstanceS:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("VehicleSeat");
				if (seat.Occupant ~= nil) then
					DestroyToy:FireServer(blobmanInstanceS);
					successCheck = false;
					break;
				end
				if ((rag.Value == true) or (held.Value == true)) then
					while ((rag.Value == true) or (held.Value == true)) and AutoGucciT do
						rs.CharacterEvents.Struggle:FireServer();
						task.wait();
					end
					successCheck = false;
					break;
				end
				blobHRP = blobmanInstanceS and blobmanInstanceS:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
				if blobHRP then
					SetNetworkOwner = rs:WaitForChild("GrabEvents"):WaitForChild("SetNetworkOwner");
					pcall(function()
						SetNetworkOwner:FireServer(blobHRP, hrp);
					end);
					blobHRP.CFrame = CFrame.new(0, 999999, 0);
				end
				task.wait();
			end
			if not successCheck then
				blobHRP = blobmanInstanceS and blobmanInstanceS:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
				v6:Notify({Title="[ 🔓 ]",Content="구찌실패 | 기다려 씨발",Duration=1,Image=nil});
				if hum then
					rs.CharacterEvents.Struggle:FireServer(plr);
					hum.Sit = true;
					task.wait(0.1);
					hum.Sit = false;
					if (blobHRP.Position.Y > 9000) then
						DestroyToy:FireServer(blobmanInstanceS);
					end
				end
				sitJumpT = false;
				task.wait(1);
			end
		end);
		task.wait();
	end
end

function HasNoLegs(v230)
	return not (v230:FindFirstChild("Left Leg") and v230:FindFirstChild("Right Leg"));
end
function StartMonitoring()
	if Monitoring then
		return;
	end
	Monitoring = true;
	task.spawn(function()
		while ToggleActive do
			char = plr.Character;
			humanoid = char and char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid");
			if (char and humanoid) then
				if HasNoLegs(char) then
					humanoid.HipHeight = 2;
				else
					repeat
						task.wait();
					until not ToggleActive or HasNoLegs(plr.Character) 
				end
			end
			task.wait();
		end
		Monitoring = false;
	end);
end
plr.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(v231)
	if ToggleActive then
		v231:WaitForChild("Humanoid");
		repeat
			task.wait(0.2);
		until HasNoLegs(v231) or not ToggleActive 
		if ToggleActive then
			StartMonitoring();
		end
	end
end);

function BlobSit()
	if BLOBSIT then
		return;
	end
	char = plr.Character;
	if not char then
		return;
	end
	humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid");
	if not humanoid then
		return;
	end
	if (humanoid.SeatPart ~= nil) then
		return;
	end
	BLOBSIT = true;
	myInv = workspace:FindFirstChild(plr.Name .. "SpawnedInToys");
	myBlob = myInv and myInv:FindFirstChild("CreatureBlobman");
	if myBlob then
		seat = myBlob:FindFirstChildOfClass("VehicleSeat");
		if seat then
			if (seat.Occupant == nil) then
				seat:Sit(humanoid);
				BLOBSIT = false;
				return;
			else
				targetPlr = game.Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(seat.Occupant.Parent);
				if targetPlr then
					TP(targetPlr);
					task.wait(0.3);
					SetOwner(targetPlr);
					task.wait(0.05);
					seat:Sit(humanoid);
					BLOBSIT = false;
					return;
				end
			end
		end
	end

function AntiExplosionF()
	if AntiExplosionC then
		AntiExplosionC:Disconnect();
		AntiExplosionC = nil;
	end
	if AntiExplosionH then
		AntiExplosionH:Disconnect();
		AntiExplosionH = nil;
	end
	if not AntiExplosionT then
		return;
	end
	local v333 = plr.Character;
	if not v333 then
		return;
	end
	local v334 = v333:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart");
	local v335 = v333:WaitForChild("Humanoid");
	AntiExplosionC = workspace.ChildAdded:Connect(function(v1254)
		if (not v333 or not v334 or not v335) then
			return;
		end
		if (v1254:IsA("BasePart") and ((v1254.Position - v334.Position).Magnitude <= 20)) then
			if (v335.SeatPart ~= nil) then
				v334.Anchored = true;
				task.wait(0.03);
				v334.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0);
				v334.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0);
				v334.Anchored = false;
			elseif (v1254:IsA("BasePart") and ((v1254.Position - v334.Position).Magnitude <= 20)) then
				v334.Anchored = true;
				task.wait();
				v335:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Running);
				v334.Anchored = false;
				v335.AutoRotate = true;
				for v3415, v3416 in ipairs(v333:GetDescendants()) do
					if (v3416:IsA("BasePart") and (v3416.Name == "RagdollLimbPart")) then
						v3416.CanCollide = false;
					end
				end
			end
		end
	end);
end

function flyF()
	if not flyT then
		return;
	end
	v2[21914] = game:GetService("Players");
	v2[21922] = game:GetService("UserInputService");
	v2[21930] = game:GetService("RunService");
	v2[21938] = v2[21914].LocalPlayer;
	v2[21944] = v2[21938].Character or v2[21938].CharacterAdded:Wait();
	local v344 = v2[21944]:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") or v2[21944]:WaitForChild("Humanoid");
	local v345 = v2[21944]:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or v2[21944]:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart");
	local v346 = Instance.new("BodyVelocity");
	local v347 = Instance.new("BodyGyro");
	v347.P = 90000;
	v347.Parent = v345;
	v346.Parent = v345;
	v347.MaxTorque = Vector3.new(8999999488, 8999999488, 8999999488);
	v347.CFrame = v345.CFrame;
	v346.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0);
	v346.MaxForce = Vector3.new(8999999488, 8999999488, 8999999488);
	local v356 = {F=0,B=0,L=0,R=0};
	local v357 = {F=0,B=0,L=0,R=0};
	local v358 = flyV;
	if flyKeyDown then
		flyKeyDown:Disconnect();
	end
	if flyKeyUp then
		flyKeyUp:Disconnect();
	end
	if flyConnection then
		flyConnection:Disconnect();
	end
	flyKeyDown = v2[21922].InputBegan:Connect(function(v1259, v1260)
		if v1260 then
			return;
		end
		if (v1259.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.W) then
			v356.F = 1;
		elseif (v1259.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.S) then
			v356.B = -1;
		elseif (v1259.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.A) then
			v356.L = -1;
		elseif (v1259.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.D) then
			v356.R = 1;
		end
	end);
	flyKeyUp = v2[21922].InputEnded:Connect(function(v1261, v1262)
		if (v1261.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.W) then
			v356.F = 0;
		elseif (v1261.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.S) then
			v356.B = 0;
		elseif (v1261.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.A) then
			v356.L = 0;
		elseif (v1261.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.D) then
			v356.R = 0;
		end
	end);
	flyConnection = v2[21930].Heartbeat:Connect(function()
		if not flyT then
			flyConnection:Disconnect();
			if flyKeyDown then
				flyKeyDown:Disconnect();
			end
			if flyKeyUp then
				flyKeyUp:Disconnect();
			end
			v346:Destroy();
			v347:Destroy();
			v344.PlatformStand = false;
			return;
		end
		v2[22449] = workspace.CurrentCamera;
		v358 = flyV;
		if (((v356.F + v356.B) ~= 0) or ((v356.L + v356.R) ~= 0)) then
			v346.Velocity = ((v2[22449].CFrame.LookVector * (v356.F + v356.B)) + ((v2[22449].CFrame * CFrame.new(v356.L + v356.R, 0, 0).p) - v2[22449].CFrame.p)) * v358;
			v357 = {F=v356.F,B=v356.B,L=v356.L,R=v356.R};
		else
			v346.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0);
		end
		v347.CFrame = v2[22449].CFrame;
	end);
end

function KillGrabF()
	while KillGrabT and task.wait() do
		v2[22930] = workspace:FindFirstChild("GrabParts");
		if not v2[22930] then
			continue;
		end
		for v1702, v1703 in ipairs(v2[22930]:GetChildren()) do
			if not KillGrabT then
				break;
			end
			if (v1703.Name ~= "GrabPart") then
				continue;
			end
			v2[22968] = v1703:FindFirstChildOfClass("WeldConstraint");
			if (not v2[22968] or not v2[22968].Part1) then
				continue;
			end
			v2[22987] = v2[22968].Part1;

				continue;
			end
			v2[23004] = game.Players:FindFirstChild(v2[22987].Parent.Name);
			if not v2[23004] then
				continue;
			end
			v2[23026] = v2[23004].Character;
			if not v2[23026] then
				continue;
			end
			v2[23037] = v2[23026]:FindFirstChild("Head");
			local v1711 = v2[23026]:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
			local v1712 = v2[23026]:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid");
			if (not v2[23037] or not v1711 or not v1712) then
				continue;
			end
			if (v1712.Health <= 0) then
				continue;
			end
			local v1713 = plr.Character;
			if not v1713 then
				continue;
			end
			local v1714 = v1713:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
			if not v1714 then
				continue;
			end
			if ((v1714.Position - v2[22987].Position).Magnitude > 30) then
				continue;
			end
			local v1715 = v2[23037]:FindFirstChild("PartOwner");
			if WhiteListMode then
				v2[23133] = false;
				for v2886, v2887 in ipairs(Whitelist) do
					if (v2887 == v2[23004].Name) then
						v2[23133] = true;
						break;
					end
				end
				if v2[23133] then
					continue;
				end
			end
			if (not v1715 or not v1715:IsA("StringValue") or (v1715.Value ~= plr.Name)) then
				pcall(function()
					game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").GrabEvents.SetNetworkOwner:FireServer(v1711, CFrame.lookAt(v1714.Position, v1711.Position));
				end);
				continue;
			end
			game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").GrabEvents.SetNetworkOwner:FireServer(v1711, CFrame.lookAt(v1714.Position, v1711.Position));
			game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").GrabEvents.DestroyGrabLine:FireServer(v1711);

			local v2257 = Instance.new("TextLabel");
			v2257.Size = UDim2.new(0, 115, 0, 18);
			v2257.Position = UDim2.new(0, 55, 0, 25);
			v2257.BackgroundTransparency = 1;
			v2257.Text = "( @" .. v2208.Name .. " )";
			v2257.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(220, 220, 220);
			v2257.TextSize = 15;
			v2257.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham;
			v2257.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left;
			v2257.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.4;
			v2257.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0);
			v2257.Parent = v2[29451];
			if (v2208.Character and v2208.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")) then
				v2[29451].Adornee = v2208.Character.HumanoidRootPart;
				v1776(v2208, v2[29451]);
			end
		end
		for v2270, v2271 in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
			if (v2271 ~= plr) then
				v1778(v2271);
			end
		end
		local v1779 = game:GetService("Players").PlayerAdded:Connect(function(v2272)
			wait(0.5);
			if (espEnabled and (v2272 ~= plr)) then
				v1778(v2272);
			end
		end);
		table.insert(connections, v1779);
		local v1780 = game:GetService("Players").PlayerRemoving:Connect(function(v2273)
			if espObjects[v2273] then
				espObjects[v2273]:Destroy();
				espObjects[v2273] = nil;
			end
		end);
		table.insert(connections, v1780);
		for v2274, v2275 in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
			if (v2275 ~= plr) then
				v2[30409] = v2275.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
					wait(0.5);
					if (espEnabled and espObjects[v2275]) then
						v2[30431] = v2275.Character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart", 2);
						if v2[30431] then
							espObjects[v2275].Adornee = v2[30431];
						end
					end
				end);
				table.insert(connections, v2[30409]);
				v2[30467] = v2275.CharacterRemoving:Connect(function()
					if (espEnabled and espObjects[v2275]) then
						espObjects[v2275].Enabled = false;
					end
				end);
				table.insert(connections, v2[30467]);
			end
		end
	else
		for v2276, v2277 in pairs(espObjects) do
			v2277:Destroy();
		end
		espObjects = {};
		for v2278, v2279 in pairs(connections) do
			v2279:Disconnect();
		end
		connections = {};
	end
end
function AntiPCLDF()
	targetValueName = "[ " .. plr.DisplayName .. " ] ( @" .. plr.Name .. " )";
	while AntiPCLDT do
		task.wait();
		if (not hasDetectedFirstTime and AntiPCLDT) then
			for v2647, v2648 in ipairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
				if (v2648.Name == "PlayerCharacterLocationDetector") then
					for v3317, v3318 in ipairs(v2648:GetChildren()) do
						if (v3318:IsA("BoolValue") and (v3318.Name == targetValueName)) then
							plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(0, 999999, 0);
							task.wait(0.1);
							plr.Character.Humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Dead);
							hasDetectedFirstTime = true;
						end
					end
				end
			end
		elseif (AntiPCLDT and hasDetectedFirstTime and plr.Character.Humanoid.Died:Connect()) then
			character = plr.Character or plr.CharacterAdded:Wait();
			CF = character:WaitForChild("Torso").CFrame;
			char = plr.CharacterAdded:Wait();
			char:WaitForChild("Humanoid"):ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Dead);
			char:WaitForChild("Torso").CFrame = CF;
			task.wait(5);
			if not AntiPCLDT then
				hasDetectedFirstTime = false;
			end
		end
	end
end
function TrSw()
	char = plr.Character;
	hrp = char.HumanoidRootPart;
	hum = char.Humanoid;
	hrp.CFrame = workspace.Map.AlwaysHereTweenedObjects.Train.Object.ObjectModel.Seat.CFrame;
	repeat
		task.wait();
	until hum.SeatPart ~= nil 
	if not inv:FindFirstChild("InstrumentGuitarLyre") then
		task.spawn(function()
			rs.MenuToys.SpawnToyRemoteFunction:InvokeServer("InstrumentGuitarLyre", CFrame.new(0, 99999, 0), Vector3.new(0, 99999, 0));
		end);
	end
	HPT = inv:WaitForChild("InstrumentGuitarLyre"):WaitForChild("HoldPart"):WaitForChild("RigidConstraint");
	repeat
		task.wait();
		if inv:FindFirstChild("InstrumentGuitarLyre") then
			task.spawn(function()
				inv:FindFirstChild("InstrumentGuitarLyre"):FindFirstChild("HoldPart"):FindFirstChild("HoldItemRemoteFunction"):InvokeServer(inv:FindFirstChild("InstrumentGuitarLyre"), char);
			end);
		end
	until HPT.Attachment1 ~= nil 
	task.wait(0.7);
	if inv:FindFirstChild("InstrumentGuitarLyre") then
		rs.MenuToys.DestroyToy:FireServer(inv:FindFirstChild("InstrumentGuitarLyre"));
	end
end
LineLagV = 50;
function LineLagF()
	for v1332, v1333 in game.Players:GetPlayers() do
		if table.find(Whitelist, v1333.Name) then
			return;
		end
	end
	while wait(0.5) and LineLagT do
		for v1781 = 0, LineLagV do
			for v2280, v2281 in ipairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
				if (v2281.Character.Torso ~= nil) then
					rs.GrabEvents.CreateGrabLine:FireServer(v2281.Character.Torso, v2281.Character.Torso.CFrame);
				end
			end
		end
	end
end

				if v1904.Value then
					for v3474, v3475 in ipairs(v678:GetChildren()) do

							v3475.Anchored = true;

							v3477.Anchored = false;
						end
					end
				end

		end
	end
end

function AntiDeathF()
	local v741;
	local v742 = 0;
	local v743 = 1;
	v741 = rs2.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
		if not _G.AntiDeathT then
			v741:Disconnect();
			return;
		end
		v2[51868] = plr.Character;
		if not v2[51868] then
			return;
		end
		local v1490 = inv:FindFirstChild("Campfire");
		if not v1490 then
			pcall(function()
				v2[51895] = cam.CFrame.Position + (cam.CFrame.LookVector * 10);
				v2[51914] = CFrame.new(v2[51895]);
				rs.MenuToys.SpawnToyRemoteFunction:InvokeServer("Campfire", v2[51914], Vector3.new(0, 0, 0));
			end);
		else
			v2[51944] = tick();
			if ((v2[51944] - v742) >= 0.15) then
				v742 = v2[51944];
				v2[51959] = Players:GetPlayers();
				v2[51966] = {};
				for v3221, v3222 in pairs(v2[51959]) do
					if ((v3222 ~= plr) and v3222.Character and v3222.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")) then
						table.insert(v2[51966], v3222.Character.HumanoidRootPart);
					end
				end
				if (#v2[51966] > 0) then
					if (v743 > #v2[51966]) then
						v743 = 1;
					end
					local v3349 = v2[51966][v743];
					if (v3349 and v1490:FindFirstChild("Hitbox")) then
						pcall(function()
							v1490.Hitbox.CFrame = v3349.CFrame;
						end);
						v743 = v743 + 1;
					end
				end
			end
		end
	end);
end

		while vu6 do
			vu5.TimePosition = 0.3;

	end
end

local v192 = v8:CreateLabel("핑: 로딩중...");
local v193 = v8:CreateLabel("FPS: 로딩중...");
local v194 = v8:CreateLabel("계정 생성일 수: 로딩중...");
local v195 = v8:CreateLabel("프리미엄 여부: 로딩중...");
local v196 = game:GetService("UserInputService");
local v197 = "PC";
if (v196.TouchEnabled and not v196.KeyboardEnabled) then
	v197 = "Mobile";
elseif (v196.GamepadEnabled and not v196.KeyboardEnabled) then
	v197 = "Console";
end
v190:Set("기기: " .. v197);
local v198 = (gethwid and gethwid()) or "지원하지 않음";
v191:Set("HWID: " .. v198);
v194:Set("계정 생성일 수: " .. plr.AccountAge .. "일");
v195:Set("프리미엄 여부: " .. (((plr.MembershipType == Enum.MembershipType.Premium) and "Yes") or "No"));
task.spawn(function()
	while task.wait(1) do
		v2[63331] = game:GetService("Stats").Network.ServerStatsItem["Data Ping"]:GetValueString();
		v192:Set("핑: " .. string.split(v2[63331], " ")[1] .. "ms");
	end
end);
task.spawn(function()
	v2[63376] = game:GetService("RunService");
	while true do
		v2[63387] = os.clock();
		v2[63376].RenderStepped:Wait();
		v2[63402] = math.floor(1 / (os.clock() - v2[63387]));
		v193:Set("FPS: " .. v2[63402]);
		task.wait(0.3);
	end
end);
